MS Sans Serif
The buttons on the toolbar at the right of the screen may also be invoked via a single keypress of an underlined letter as indicated on the button.  For example, typing "S" is the same as pressing the size button with the mouse.
There are two exceptions to this rule.  To print, CTRL and "P" must be pressed at the same time.  Also, to exit without printing ALT and "X" must be pressed at the same time.
List of Commands
S - Size
C - Center on paper
P - Portrait mode
L - Landscape mode
T - Printer Setup
CTRL + P - Exit and Print
H - Help
ALT + X - Exit w/o printing
3 - Set to 3"x5"
4 - Set to 4"x5"
5 - Set to 5"x7"
A - Size to Page

The lettering is not in a compatible format for Month/Day/Year justification.
Lettering must be in the following format: MONTH DAY YEAR.
For example: May 6, 1997 or Oct. 25 19115The primary size must not equal 0.  Please try again.7The secondary size must not equal 0.  Please try again.
The lettering is not in a compatible format for Split justification.
Lettering must be in one of the the following formats: YEAR - YEAR or YEAR -
For example: 1997 - 1999 or 1926 - 
I am setting the justification of this line to Center.@The justify radius must be greater than zero.  Please try again.
Their is more than one line in this group.  Arc justified lines can only exist by themselves.  The Arc justified line in this group is being Center justified.FA line of lettering must be 0 or greater in length.  Please try again.
The lettering is not in a compatible format for Missouri justification.

The lettering is not in a compatible format for Split justification.
Split justified lines take one of three formats.
Format One: A Dash separates a pair of years
For example: 1997 - 1999 or 1926 -
Format Two: An underscore marks where a component will be placed.
For example: 1997_1999
Format Three: Three words on one line.
